    // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n147:     // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n148:     double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n149:     double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n150:     double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n151:     CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n152:     CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n153:     FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n154:         FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n163:         .build();\n164:   }\n165: \n166:   //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n167:   @ImmutableValidator\n168: option).\\n40:  * <p>\\n41:  * Depending on the barrier defined in {@link Barrier}, the options are classified into four types: up-and-in,\\n42:  * down-and-in, up-and-out and down-and-out.\\n43:  * <p>\\n44:  * For example, an up-and-out call on a 'EUR 1.00 / USD -1.41' exchange with barrier of 1.5 is the option to\\n45:  * perform a foreign exchange on the expiry date, where USD 1.41 is paid to is a financial instrument that provides an option to exchange two currencies at a specified future time\n39:  * only when barrier event occurs (knock-in option) or does not occur (knock-out option).\n40:  * <p>\n41:  * Depending on the barrier defined in {@link Barrier}, the options are classified into four types: up-and-in,\n42:  * down-and-in, up-and-out and down-and-out.\n43:  * <p>\n44:  * For example, an up-and-out call on a 'EUR 1.00 / USD -1.41' exchange with barrier of 1.5 is the option to\n45:  * perform a foreign exchange on the expiry date, where USD 1.41 is paid to option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   * @return an equivalent fx european option\n   */\n  public static FxEuropeanOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a european call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a european put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxEuropeanOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n        .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n        .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a european put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxEuropeanOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n
